            WHERE [r0].[RequestId] = @__requestId_1), N'')
        ELSE N'Provider ' + COALESCE((
            SELECT TOP(1) [p].[FirstName]
            FROM [Physician] AS [p]
            WHERE [p].[PhysicianId] = [r].[PhysicianId]), N'')
    END
    ELSE N'Admin ' + COALESCE((
        SELECT TOP(1) [a].[FirstName]
        FROM [Admin] AS [a]
        WHERE [a].[AdminId] = [r].[AdminId]), N'')
END AS [Uploader]
FROM [RequestWiseFile] AS [r]
WHERE [r].[RequestId] = @__requestId_0 AND [r].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)

    WHEN [r].[Status] > CAST(10 AS smallint) OR [r].[Status] < CAST(1 AS smallint) THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
END, [r].[CreatedDate]
FROM [Request] AS [r]
